                  </form> (S, K, &amp;c.) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-1" target="جُمَلٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6346"/></foreign> and

      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-3" target="جُمُلٌ" n="3" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6347"/></foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-4" target="جَمَلٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6345"/></foreign> (IJ, K) [<hi rend="ital">A cable;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">the rope of a ship,</hi> (S, K,) i. e., the <hi rend="ital">thick rope thereof,</hi> (TA,) <hi rend="ital">that is also called</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">قَلْسٌ</foreign>, (S, TA,) <hi rend="ital">consisting of</hi> [<hi rend="ital">a number of</hi>] <hi rend="ital">ropes put together:</hi> (S:) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-5" target="جُمَالَةٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> also signifies [the same; or] <hi rend="ital">a thick rope,</hi> because <hi rend="ital">consisting of many strands put together;</hi> pl. <foreign lang="ar">جُمَالَاتٌ</foreign>; (Zj, TA;) which Mujáhid explains as meaning the <hi rend="ital">ropes of bridges;</hi> but I 'Ab, as the <hi rend="ital">ropes of ships, put together so as to be like the waists of men</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in thickness</hi>]. (TA.) In all the forms mentioned above, except the last (<foreign lang="ar">جمالة</foreign>), the word is read in the phrase [in the Kur vii. 38], <foreign lang="ar">حَتَّى يَلِجَ الجُمَّلُ فِى سَمِّ الخِيَاطِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Until the cable shall enter into the eye of the needle</hi>]: (K, TA:) I 'Ab reads <foreign lang="ar">الجُمَّلُ</foreign>, (S, TA,) and so do 'Alee and many others:   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-6" target="جُمْلٌ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6344"/></foreign> is pl. [or rather coll. gen. n.] of <foreign lang="ar">جُمْلَةٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">a strand</hi> of a thick rope; or, accord. to IJ, pl. of <foreign lang="ar">جَمَلٌ</foreign> [q. v.]: the first is explained by Fr as meaning <hi rend="ital">ropes put together;</hi> but Aboo-Tálib thinks that he meant   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-7" target="جُمَلٌ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n6346"/></foreign>, without tesh-deed. (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">حِسَابُ الجُمَّلِ</foreign>, (S K,) thought by IDrd to be not Arabic, (TA,) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n6360-8" target="الجُمَلِ" n="8" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, (K,) but IDrd doubts its correctness, <hi rend="ital">The calculation by means of the letters</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">د ج ب ا</foreign>, &amp;c. (TA.)    </entryFree>30:T82d,<entryFree id="n6363" key="جَامِلٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">جَامِلٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">جامل</orth>
                  </form> [act. part. n. of <foreign lang="ar">جَمَلَ</foreign>.       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  And also part. n. of <foreign lang="ar">جَمُلَ</foreign>]. The Arabs say, <foreign lang="ar">اُجْمُلْ إِنْ كُنْتَ جَامِلًا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Become beautiful,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">if thou be becoming beautiful,</hi> &amp;c.]: but when they mean the quality [alone], they say, <foreign lang="ar">إِنَّهُ لَجَمِيلٌ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Verily he is beautiful,</hi> &amp;c.]. (Lh, TA.)       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  A man <hi rend="ital">possessing a</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">جَمَل</foreign> [or <hi rend="ital">he-camel</hi>]. (TA. [See also <foreign lang="ar">جَمَّالٌ</foreign>.])          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">A herd,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">distinct number, of camels,</hi> (S, K, * TA,) <hi rend="ital">males and females,</hi> (TA,) <hi rend="ital">with their pastors and their owners:</hi> (S, K, TA: [also said in the K to be a pl. of <foreign lang="ar">جَمَلٌ</foreign>: in the CK, <foreign lang="ar">الجامِعُ</foreign> is erroneously put for <foreign lang="ar">الجَامِلُ</foreign>:]) or a word formed to denote a pl., meaning <hi rend="ital">camels,</hi> (Ham pp. 122 and 490,) <hi rend="ital">males and females;</hi> (Id p. 122;) derived from <foreign lang="ar">جَمَلٌ</foreign>; (Id. p. 490;) like <foreign lang="ar">بَاقِرٌ</foreign> (Id. ib. and TA) from <foreign lang="ar">بَقَرٌ</foreign>, (Ham p. 490,) and <foreign lang="ar">كَالِبٌ</foreign> [from <foreign lang="ar">كَلْبٌ</foreign>]. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">A great tribe.</hi> (AHeyth, K.)
